msg:I stayed at the Zhongzhou Huading Hotel in Dengfeng for five nights. I am very satisfied with the hotel, using the Henan dialect to express my feelings. The hotel is close to the Zhongyue Temple, with convenient transportation. The hotel has a good environment inside and outside. The rooms are square and spacious, the service is thoughtful (lobby, concierge, restaurant, guest room, everywhere), the breakfast is diverse and nutritious, and every day is very smooth, down-to-earth and comfortable. I can't find any faults. I would like to thank the following three things in particular:
1) Thank you for the help of Ms. Zhang Lishan, the assistant manager of the hotel lobby, who upgraded the room to a mountain view room (I personally like quietness). The balcony overlooks the Zhongyue Temple and Huanggai Peak under the Taishi Mountain. Whether it is sunny or rainy, the scenery is very pleasant.
2) After checking in, I found that Dengfeng has stopped heating in the past few days. Thank you for letting Ms. Wang from the housekeeping depar**ent provide the room with an oil heater at the first time to warm my body and heart.
3) It happened to be my birthday when I checked out. I am grateful to Ms. Zhang Lishan for noticing it and giving me a gift on behalf of the hotel (a flying dragon doll and a little monk ornament). I didn't expect the hotel service to be so meticulous. I was so surprised that I couldn't control my expression and my eyes seemed to be red.
I have been to Dengfeng three times, and I have been surprised every time. I hope I will have the opportunity to visit Songshan Mountain in Dengfeng again and stay at Zhongzhou Huading again in the future. I am happy! ! !
